     <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Transportation">\n        Transportation\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Delray_Beach,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Transportation">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Highways">\n        Highways\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Delray_Beach,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Highways">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Florida_A1A.svg">\n         <img alt="Florida A1A.svg" data-file-height="601" data-file-width="751" height="19" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Florida_A1A.svg/24px-Florida_A1A.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Florida_A1A.svg/36px-Florida_A1A.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Florida_A1A.svg/48px-Florida_A1A.svg.png 2x" width="24"/>\n        </a>\n        <a href="/wiki/Florida_State_Road_A1A" title="Florida State Road A1A">\n         Florida State Road A1A\n        </a>\n        , locally known as "Ocean Boulevard", is a north-south Scenic and Historic Coastal Byway passing through the city between the Intracoastal Waterway and the Atlantic Ocean.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:US_1.svg">\n         <img alt="US 1.svg" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="600" height="24" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/US_1.svg/24px-US_1.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/US_1.svg/36px-US_1.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/US_1.svg/48px-US_1.svg.png 2x" width="24"/>\n        </a>\n        <a href="/wiki/U.S._Route_1_in_Florida" title="U.S. Route 1 in Florida">\n         U.S. Route 1\n        </a>\n        , also known as "Federal Highway", is a north\xe2\x80\x93south road passing through downtown, commercial districts, and residential areas in the eastern part of the city. US1 splits into a divided\n        <a href="/wiki/One-way_pair" title="One-way pair">\n         one-way pair\n        </a>\n        through downtown.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:I-95.svg">\n         <img alt="I-95.svg" data-file-height="601" data-file-width="601" height="24" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/I-95.svg/24px-I-95.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/I-95.svg/36px-I-95.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/I-95.svg/48px-I-95.svg.png 2x" width="24"/>\n        </a>\n        <a href="/wiki/Interstate_95_in_Florida" title="Interstate 95 in Florida">\n         Interstate 95\n        </a>\n        bisects the city from north to south with two Delray Beach interchanges.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Florida%27s_Turnpike_shield.png">\n         <img alt="Florida\'s Turnpike shield.png" data-file-height="277" data-file-width="232" height="29" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Florida%27s_Turnpike_shield.png/24px-Florida%27s_Turnpike_shield.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Florida%27s_Turnpike_shield.png/36px-Florida%27s_Turnpike_shield.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Florida%27s_Turnpike_shield.png/48px-Florida%27s_Turnpike_shield.png 2x" width="24"/>\n        </a>\n        <a href="/wiki/Florida%27s_Turnpike" title="Florida\'s Turnpike">\n         Florida\'s Turnpike\n        </a>\n        is a north-south\n        <a href="/wiki/Toll_road" title="Toll road">\n         toll road\n        </a>\n        passing through unincorporated Delray Beach, with an interchange at Atlantic Avenue.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:US_441.svg">\n         <img alt="US 441.svg" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="750" height="19" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/US_441.svg/24px-US_441.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/US_441.svg/36px-US_441.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/US_441.svg/48px-US_441.svg.png 2x" width="24"/>\n        </a>\n        <a href="/wiki/U.S._Route_441_in_Florida" title="U.S. Route 441 in Florida">\n         U.S. Highway 441\n        </a>\n        , also known as\n        <a href="/wiki/Florida_State_Road_7" title="Florida State Road 7">\n         State Road 7\n        </a>\n        , is a north-south highway passing through residential and commercial areas west of the city limits.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Other major north-south roads include\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Florida_State_Road_807" title="Florida State Road 807">\n         Congress Avenue\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Florida_State_Road_809" title="Florida State Road 809">\n         Military Trail\n        </a>\n        , and\n        <a href="/wiki/Florida_State_Road_845" title="Florida State Road 845">\n         Jog Road\n        </a>\n        .\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Florida_806.svg">\n         <img alt="Florida 806.svg" data-file-height="601" data-file-width="751" height="19" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Florida_806.svg/24px-Florida_806.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Florida_806.svg/36px-Florida_806.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Florida_806.svg/48px-Florida_806.svg.png 2x" width="24"/>\n        </a>\n        <a href="/wiki/Florida_State_Road_806" title="Florida State Road 806">\n         Florida State Road 806\n        </a>\n        , locally known as "Atlantic Avenue", is the primary east\xe2\x80\x93west route between State Road A1A and US 441, and the central commercial thoroughfare downtown.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Atlantic Avenue, Linton Boulevard, and George Bush Boulevard are the east-west roads with\n        <a href="/wiki/Moveable_bridge" title="Moveable bridge">\n         drawbridge\n        </a>\n        crossings over the Intracoastal Waterway.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Rail">\n        Rail\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Delray_Beach,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Rail">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Tri-Rail" title="Tri-Rail">\n         Tri-Rail\n        </a>\n        commuter rail system and\n        <a href="/wiki/Amtrak" title="Amtrak">\n         Amtrak\n        </a>\n        serve the city with stops at\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Delray_Beach_(Tri-Rail_station)" title="Delray Beach (Tri-Rail station)">\n         Delray Beach Station\n        </a>\n        .\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">\n         <a href="#cite_note-113">\n          [113]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114">\n         <a href="#cite_note-114">\n          [114]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Bus">\n        Bus\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Delray_Beach,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Bus">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/PalmTran" title="PalmTran">\n         PalmTran\n        </a>\n        provides local bus service in the area.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">\n         <a href="#cite_note-115">\n          [115]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Shuttle">\n        Shuttle\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Delray_Beach,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Shuttle">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        The Downtown Roundabout: A free shuttle that connects the Tri-Rail Station to Downtown Delray Beach. With two routes, and 22 stops throughout the downtown, it operates 7 days a week.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">\n         <a href="#cite_note-116">\n          [116]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The Downtowner: An on-demand, local, free ride service utilizing green technology.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117">\n         <a href="#cite_note-117">\n          [117]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Water">\n        Water\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Delray_Beach,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Water">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Downtown Delray Beach is accessible by boat via The Intracoastal Waterway. The city has a municipal marina with rental slips just south of the Atlantic Avenue crossing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-City_Marina_108-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-City_Marina-108">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Yacht cruises also launch daily from Veteran\'s Park just north of the Atlantic Avenue drawbridge.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">\n        <a href="#cite_note-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_people">\n
